self = <queue3.DoublyLinkedList object at 0x7fa6f820f670>, value = '[]'

    def addAtHead(self, value: T) -> None:
    
        """Add node at head end."""
    
        if self.__size < 0:
            newNode = Node(value)
            self.__sentinel.next = newNode
            newNode.prev = self.__sentinel
            self.__tail = newNode
            self.__size += 1
